<Z>Christmas Hours <C> The office will close at the end of Thursday 22nd December. Turns due that day will run on time, in the<L.31.1>
hope they reach you by Christmas Eve. Aside from a round of Gridstats (due Tuesday 27th December) I'll then be closed until<L.31.1>
Tuesday 3rd January 2006, which effectively means one week off running games (week beginning Monday 26th December).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Recruiting <C> In the past we've offered a couple of free credits if you introduce someone new to one of our games. I'm now<L.31.1>
going to increase this "bounty" to five credits. It's becoming harder and harder to persuade new people to play PBM games, so it<L.31.1>
makes to try and increase the reward to encourage you guys to try and find more people to play the games, providing us with<L.31.1>
customers and you with opponents! Please be clear that this bonus is for recruiting NEW players - persuading someone to leave one<L.31.1>
league to join another, or move to Raceplan from Gameplan doesn't count. If you're on a chat forum for fans of your sport, or a<L.31.1>
member of a fan club and so forth, then preach the gospel and if people mention you when they join, we'll add the credits.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Late Email Results <C> If you think results are late, please make sure you wait until the following morning before chasing up<L.31.1>
results. First step is to check out the Latest News at www.pbmsports.com - if I am running late I'll post a notice there. If not,<L.31.1>
then drop me a line, but please do wait until that next morning - emails aren't always instant and just because you know someone<L.31.1>
else who got their results doesn't mean yours won't show up - emails can take a few hours to get through.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>PDF Reports <C> Emailed game reports in Gameplan Baseball, Raceplan, Hoopplan, Slapshot, Gridstats and Soccer Stats are now<L.31.1>
available as PDF files. Other games will follow as we get them programmed (so please be patient).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
I won't change your game reports from "Text" to "PDF" until you ask me to, and if you want a trial of a PDF report let me know.<L.31.1>
You should find PDF reports rather easier to cope with - Adobe Reader is free to download (see www.pbmsports.com for a link) and<L.31.1>
you can open your reports with one click of the mouse (indeed, you don't need a printer, though most of you will then print from<L.31.1>
it) and you don't need to worry about dodgy email clients (Hotmail and AOL are particularly common culprits) messing up the<L.31.1>
formatting, or printer drivers. If you want to stay with the text format that's fine but I only expect people will want to do so<L.31.1>
if they use the text file for other purposes (such as exporting the listings into some software you've produced yourself).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
If you've not tried email reports before, or you've had problems, try out the PDF. It really is very straightforward.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>

Dollars or Aussie Dollars, whichever you prefer. Cheques are still fine as well, and actually mean slightly lower charges for us!<L.31.1>
